# LLVM Optimization Pass Pipeline Propagation

## Your Task

Trace how an LLVM optimization pass is registered in the pass pipeline and executed. Find all C++ source files in `llvm/llvm-project` that participate in the optimization pipeline lifecycle: 1. The file that defines the `PassBuilder` class and its method for building the default O2 optimization pipeline (look in `llvm/lib/Passes/`). 2. The file that defines the `PassManager` template class — the core pass execution engine (look in `llvm/include/llvm/IR/`). 3. The file that implements `PassBuilderPipelines` which assembles the default module/function simplification pipelines. 4. The file that registers all standard passes via `PassRegistry.def`. 5. For a concrete example, the file implementing `DeadStoreElimination` in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Scalar/`. Report the repo, file path, and key class or function name for each.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

{"content":"1: //===- DeadStoreElimination.cpp - MemorySSA Backed Dead Store Elimination -===//\n2: //\n3: // Part of the LLVM Project, under the Apache License v2.0 with LLVM Exceptions.\n4: // See https://llvm.org/LICENSE.txt for license information.\n5: // SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0 WITH LLVM-exception\n6: //\n7: //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n8: //\n9: // The code below implements dead store elimination using MemorySSA. Then check\n12: // that there are no uses that may read the location of the original MemoryDef\n13: // in between both MemoryDefs. ## Summary

I've identified all the key components in the LLVM optimization pass pipeline lifecycle:

### **Key Files Found:**

1. **PassBuilder** (`llvm/include/llvm/Passes/PassBuilder.h` and `llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilder.cpp`)
   - Contains the `PassBuilder` class that orchestrates pipeline construction
   - Key method: `buildModuleOptimizationPipeline()` for building O2 optimization pipelines

2. **PassManager Template** (`llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManager.h`)
   - Core template class `PassManager<IRUnitT, AnalysisManagerT, ExtraArgTs...>` (lines 159-226)
   - Typedefs: `ModulePassManager` and `FunctionPassManager`
   - Implements the `run()` method that executes all passes in sequence

3. **PassBuilderPipelines** (`llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilderPipelines.cpp`)
   - Implements the actual pipeline construction logic
   - `buildModuleOptimizationPipeline()` assembles default module/function simplification pipelines

4. **PassRegistry** (`llvm/lib/Passes/PassRegistry.def`)
   - Central registry of all standard passes using macros
   - Includes entries like `FUNCTION_PASS("dse", DSEPass())`

5. **DeadStoreElimination** - Concrete example pass:
   - Header: `llvm/include/llvm/Transforms/Scalar/DeadStoreElimination.h` - defines `DSEPass` class
   - Implementation: `llvm/lib/Transforms/Scalar/DeadStoreElimination.cpp` - actual optimization algorithm

It uses\n10: // the following general approach: given a MemoryDef, walk upwards to find\n11: // clobbering MemoryDefs that may be killed by the starting def. Then check\n12: // that there are no uses that may read the location of the original MemoryDef\n13: // in between both MemoryDefs. StartDef is executed whenever CurrentDef is executed.\n25: //   3. StartDef completely overwrites CurrentDef.\n26: // 4.
